				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Ein feste Burg ist unser Gott, BWV 80 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div id="contentSub">(Redirected from <a href="/index.php?title=Alles,_was_von_Gott_geboren,_BWV_80a_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)&amp;redirect=no" title="Alles, was von Gott geboren, BWV 80a (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Alles, was von Gott geboren, BWV 80a (Bach, Johann Sebastian)</a>)</div><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1727-31, rev. 1744-47
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Ein feste Burg ist unser Gott
</td></tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>
<td><span title="fr, pt, de">Ein feste Burg ist unser Gott (Bach)</span>; <span title="nl">A Mighty Fortress Is Our God</span>; <span title="nl">Eine feste Burg ist unser Gott</span>; <span title="pt, de">BWV 80</span>; <span title="nn">Ein' feste Burg ist unser Gott</span>; <span title="ja">我らが神は堅き砦</span>

<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 80/a-b&#160;; BC A 52/183 a-b
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 106
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>D major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 movements:
<ol><li>Chorus: Ein feste Burg ist unser Gott (D&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (soprano, bass): Alles, was von Gott geboren (D&#160;major)
</li><li>Recitativo (bass): Erwäge doch (B&#160;minor-F<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266f;</span>&#160;minor)
</li><li>Aria (soprano): Komm in mein Herzenhaus (B&#160;minor)
</li><li>Chorus: Und wenn die Welt voll Teufel wär (D&#160;major)
</li><li>Recitativo (tenor): So stehe dann (B&#160;minor-D&#160;major)
</li><li>Duetto (alto, tenor): Wie selig sind doch die, die Gott im Munde tragen (G&#160;major)
</li><li>Chorale: Das Wort sie sollen lassen stahn (D&#160;major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1727-31, rev. 1744-47
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
